 0 naam ke khatarnaak virus ne android divaais main dobaaraa dastak de di he
 Significantly, this bug has been exposed by this security startup
 security exparts ke mutabik yah virus phir se android main aana shuru ho gaya he or philhal 1 billian android divaais isse prabhavit hai
 How Stagefright Bug Works Hackers send MMS to your smartphone through this bug
 ise risive karne ke baad ve aapke smartphone ko puri tarah control kar sakate hai
 This bug penetrates your device through the smartphone's Mp3 and Mp4
 padhein: aise bachaaen smartphone ko virus cesecority research mark james ke mutabik, mobile se kisi website par aap jaise hi koi video yaa gaanaa sunne ke liye clic karte hai vaise hi ataikar aapke mobile ko remoteli control karnaa shuru kar detaa he

 kya he stagefrightstagefright kaa pehla maamla 2003 main saamne aayaa tha
 This is a bug created by hackers that attacks the media processing system of Android devices

 On the Manikarnika Ghat of Kashi, after the death, the dead are brought in search of salvation, while on the other side, all these municipalities come to achieve salvation by winning
 wo moksh jo inhen agle janm main nagarvadhoona banane kaayakin dilaataa he

 jo jitani hairaan karne vaali he usase kahin zyaadapareshaan karne vaali
 The tradition of the dance of the townspeople amidst the silence of the crematorium is hundreds of years old
 manyataon ke mutabik aaj se saikadon saal pehle raja maan sinhadvarabanaae gaebaba mashaan nath ke darbar main kaaryakam pesh karne ke liye us samay ke jane-maane nartkiyon or kalakaaron ko bulaayaa gaya tha lekin chunki ye mandir shmashaan ghat ke bichon bich maujuud tha, lihaaja tab cachoti ke tamaam kalakaaron ne yahaan aakar apane kala kaa johar dikhaane se inkaar kar diya tha

 feechar phone par itnaa jor dene ke bare main puche jane par agarwal ne kaha, ‘‘desh kii ek badi aabaadi abhi bhi feechar phone pasand kar rahi he

 iske liye ham 20 karod rapaye ke nivesh se ek nayaa kaarkaana laga rahe hai jo agle vitt varsh 2017-18 kii shuruuaat se puri tarah kaam karne lagegaa

 vah bhartiya cinema ko ek nai oonchai par le gaye hai

 nyaayamurti manmohan ne susheel ke vakil se poocha, 'bhartiya kushti mahasang kii niti lambey samay se chali aa rahi he or ab aap kah rahe hai ki yah galat he
 "he said," Sushil went to the Olympics three times in 2004, 2008 and 2012 based on this policy
 mahasang kii niti tabhi se chali aa rahi hai
 On behalf of Sushil, Senior Advocate Amit Sibal told the court that the Wrestling Federation of India should follow the Code of Conduct and there should be selection trials for international tournaments like the Olympics

 Judicial First Class Magistrate NR Gajbhiye of Dharmabad in Nanded district directed the police to arrest all the accused and produce them in court by 21 September
 tippaniyan Naidu and others, then in opposition in undivided Andhra Pradesh, were arrested for protesting near the Babli project in Maharashtra and were jailed in Pune
 ve is aadhaar par pariyojna kaa virodh kar rahe the ki isse nichle hisse main log prabhavit honge

 un sabhi par janasevak ko kaam karne main baadha pahunchane ke liye hamalaa yaa aapraadhik bal prayog karne, hathiyaar yaa kisi anya tareeke se jaanboojhkar jakhm pahunchaana, anya kii jindagi khatre main daalane samet bhadansan kii vibhinn dharaaen lagaayi gayi hai

 baad main unhen reeha kar diya gaya tha lekin unhone jamaanat nahin maangi thi
 All of them have been charged with various sections of conspiracy, including assault or using criminal force, deliberately inflicting injuries by weapons or any other means, to endanger the lives of others to hinder public servants

 (from input language) naagarikta sanshodhan bill ko cabinet kii manjuuri sambhavajald hi sansad main pesh kiya jayega naagarikta billpurvottar main kai dal kar rahe hai bill kaa virodhrashtriya naagarikta register (NRC) ko lekar abhi purvottar main bavaal thama bhi nahin tha ki centre sarkaar naagarikta sanshodhan bill le ai
 The bill was also passed by the Rajya Sabha on Wednesday
 somvaar ko ise loksabhaa se bhi paas kiya gaya tha
 With the change in the bill, many rules of citizenship to refugees settled in India will be changed, which the opposition is opposing
 is bill main kya khaas he, kis par vipaksh virodh kar rahaa he or kya badlaav hone ja rahe hai, yahaan samajhen
 
 
 1
 naagarikta sanshodhan bill kya he?jo bill sansad se paas hua he, vah naagarikta adhinium 1955 main badlaav karegaa
 Under this, citizens of Hindu, Sikh, Buddhist, Jain, Zoroastrian religion coming to India from nearby countries including Bangladesh, Pakistan, Afghanistan will be given citizenship
 2
 How will it be easy to get citizenship of India? After this bill is converted into law, non-muslim refugees from countries like Afghanistan, Bangladesh, Pakistan will come to India, it will become easier to get citizenship here
 iske liye unhen bharat main kam se kam 6 saal bitaane honge
 The first citizenship grant was over 11 years
 3
 What is being opposed on the bill? Opposition is besieging the central government about this bill, in which the main opposition is about religion
 nae sanshodhan bill main muslimon ko chhodkar anya dharmon ke logon ko aasaani se naagarikta dene par faisla kiya ja rahaa he
 The Opposition is raising this point and is describing this decision of the Modi government on the basis of religion
